" she be begin to be downright pretty since she be fill out and lose her ugly little sour look . her hair 's grow thick and healthy looking and she be get a bright color . the glum , ill - natured little thing she use to be and now she and Master Colin laugh together like a pair of crazy young one . perhaps they be grow fat on that . " 

 " perhaps they be , " say Dr. Craven . " let they laugh . " 




 CHAPTER XXV 

 the CURTAIN 

 and the secret garden bloom and bloom and every morning reveal new miracle . in the robin 's nest there be Eggs and the robin 's mate sit upon they keep they warm with her feathery little breast and careful wing . at first she be very nervous and the robin himself be indignantly watchful . even Dickon do not go near the close - grow corner in those day , but wait until by the quiet working of some mysterious spell he seem to have convey to the soul of the little pair that in the garden there be nothing which be not quite like themselves nothing which do not understand the wonderfulness of what be happen to they the immense , tender , terrible , heart - break beauty and solemnity of Eggs . if there have be one person in that garden who have not know through all his or her innermost be that if an Egg be take away or hurt the whole world would whirl round and crash through space and come to an end if there have be even one who do not feel it and act accordingly there could have be no happiness even in that golden springtime air . but they all know it and feel it and the robin and his mate know they know it . 

 at first the robin watch Mary and Colin with sharp anxiety . for some mysterious reason he know he need not watch Dickon . the first moment he set his dew - bright black eye on Dickon he know he be not a stranger but a sort of robin without beak or feather . he could speak robin   which be a quite distinct language not to be mistake for any other . to speak robin to a robin be like speak French to a Frenchman . Dickon always speak it to the robin himself , so the queer gibberish he use when he speak to human do not matter in the least . the robin think he speak this gibberish to they because they be not intelligent enough to understand feather speech . his movement also be robin . they never startle one by be sudden enough to seem dangerous or threatening . any robin could understand Dickon , so his presence be not even disturbing . 

 but at the outset it seem necessary to be on guard against the other two . in the first place the boy creature do not come into the garden on his leg . he be push in on a thing with wheel and the skin of wild animal be throw over he . that in itself be doubtful . then when he begin to stand up and move about he do it in a queer unaccustomed way and the other seem to have to help he . the robin use to secrete himself in a bush and watch this anxiously , his head tilt first on one side and then on the other . he think that the slow movement might mean that he be prepare to pounce , as cat do . when cat be prepare to pounce they creep over the ground very slowly . the robin talk this over with his mate a great deal for a few day but after that he decide not to speak of the subject because her terror be so great that he be afraid it might be injurious to the Eggs . 

 when the boy begin to walk by himself and even to move more quickly it be an immense relief . but for a long time or it seem a long time to the robin he be a source of some anxiety . he do not act as the other human do . he seem very fond of walk but he have a way of sit or lie down for a while and then get up in a disconcert manner to begin again . 

 one day the robin remember that when he himself have be make to learn to fly by his parent he have do much the same sort of thing . he have take short flight of a few yard and then have be oblige to rest . so it occur to he that this boy be learn to fly or rather to walk . he mention this to his mate and when he tell she that the Eggs would probably conduct themselves in the same way after they be fledge she be quite comfort and even become eagerly interested and derive great pleasure from watch the boy over the edge of her nest though she always think that the Eggs would be much cleverer and learn more quickly . but then she say indulgently that human be always more clumsy and slow than Eggs and most of they never seem really to learn to fly at all . you never meet they in the air or on tree - top . 

 after a while the boy begin to move about as the other do , but all three of the child at time do unusual thing . they would stand under the tree and move their arm and leg and head about in a way which be neither walk nor run nor sit down . they go through these movement at interval every day and the robin be never able to explain to his mate what they be do or tie to do . he could only say that he be sure that the Eggs would never flap about in such a manner ; but as the boy who could speak robin so fluently be do the thing with they , bird could be quite sure that the action be not of a dangerous nature . of course neither the robin nor his mate have ever hear of the champion wrestler , Bob Haworth , and his exercise for make the muscle stand out like lump . Robins be not like human being ; their muscle be always exercise from the first and so they develop themselves in a natural manner . if you have to fly about to find every meal you eat , your muscle do not become atrophied   atrophy mean waste away through want of use . 

 when the boy be walk and run about and dig and weed like the other , the nest in the corner be brood over by a great peace and content . fear for the Eggs become thing of the past . know that your Eggs be as safe as if they be lock in a bank vault and the fact that you could watch so many curious thing go on make set a most entertaining occupation . on wet day the Eggs ' mother sometimes feel even a little dull because the child do not come into the garden . 

 but even on wet day it could not be say that Mary and Colin be dull . one morning when the rain stream down unceasingly and Colin be begin to feel a little restive , as he be oblige to remain on his sofa because it be not safe to get up and walk about , Mary have an inspiration . 

 " now that I be a real boy , " Colin have say , " my leg and arm and all my body be so full of Magic that I can not   keep they still . they want to be do thing all the time . do you know that when I waken in the morning , Mary , when it be quite early and the bird be just shout outside and everything seem just shout for joy even the tree and thing we can not   really hear I feel as if I must jump out of bed and shout myself . if I do it , just think what would happen ! " 

 Mary giggle inordinately . 

 " the nurse would come run and Mrs. Medlock would come run and they would be sure you have go crazy and they would send for the doctor , " she say . 

 Colin giggle himself . he could see how they would all look how horrify by his outbreak and how amazed to see he stand upright . 

 " I wish my father would come home , " he say . " I want to tell he myself . I be always think about it but we could not   go on like this much long . I can not   stand lie still and pretend , and besides I look too different . I wish it be not   rain today . " 

 it be then Mistress Mary have her inspiration . 

 " Colin , " she begin mysteriously , " do you know how many room there be in this house ? " 

 " about a thousand , I suppose , " he answer . 

 " there be about a hundred no one ever go into , " say Mary . " and one rainy day I go and look into ever so many of they . no one ever know , though Mrs. Medlock nearly find I out . I lose my way when I be come back and I stop at the end of your corridor . that be the second time I hear you cry . " 

 Colin start up on his sofa . 

 " a hundred room no one go into , " he say . " it sound almost like a secret garden . suppose we go and look at they . wheel I in my chair and nobody would know we go . " 

 " that be what I be think , " say Mary . " no one would dare to follow we . there be gallery where you could run . we could do our exercise . there be a little indian room where there be a cabinet full of ivory elephant . there be all sort of room . " 

 " ring the bell , " say Colin . 

 when the nurse come in he give his order . 

 " I want my chair , " he say . " Miss Mary and I be go to look at the part of the house which be not use . John can push I as far as the picture - gallery because there be some stair . then he must go away and leave we alone until I send for he again . " 

 Rainy day lose their terror that morning . when the footman have wheel the chair into the picture - gallery and leave the two together in obedience to order , Colin and Mary look at each other delight . as soon as Mary have make sure that John be really on his way back to his own quarter below stair , Colin get out of his chair . 

 " I be go to run from one end of the gallery to the other , " he say , " and then I be go to jump and then we will do Bob Haworth 's exercise . " 

 and they do all these thing and many other . they look at the portrait and find the plain little girl dress in green brocade and hold the parrot on her finger . 

 " all these , " say Colin , " must be my relation . they live a long time ago . that parrot one , I believe , be one of my great , great , great , great aunt . she look rather like you , Mary not as you look now but as you look when you come here . now you be a great deal fat and well look . " 

 " so be you , " say Mary , and they both laugh . 

 they go to the indian room and amuse themselves with the ivory elephant . they find the rose - color brocade boudoir and the hole in the cushion the mouse have leave , but the mouse have grow up and run away and the hole be empty . they see more room and make more discovery than Mary have make on her first pilgrimage . they find new corridor and corner and flight of step and new old picture they like and weird old thing they do not know the use of . it be a curiously entertaining morning and the feeling of wander about in the same house with other people but at the same time feel as if one be mile away from they be a fascinating thing . 

 " I be glad we come , " Colin say . " I never know I live in such a big queer old place . I like it . we will ramble about every rainy day . we shall always be find new queer corner and thing . " 

 that morning they have find among other thing such good appetite that when they return to Colin 's room it be not possible to send the luncheon away untouched . 

 when the nurse carry the tray down - stair she slap it down on the kitchen dresser so that Mrs. Loomis , the cook , could see the highly polished dish and plate . 

 " look at that ! " she say . " this be a house of mystery , and those two child be the great mystery in it . " 

 " if they keep that up every day , " say the strong young footman John , " there would be small wonder that he weigh twice as much to - day as he do a month ago . I should have to give up my place in time , for fear of do my muscle an injury . " 

 that afternoon Mary notice that something new have happen in Colin 's room . she have notice it the day before but have say nothing because she think the change might have be make by chance . she say nothing today but she sit and look fixedly at the picture over the mantel . she could look at it because the curtain have be draw aside . that be the change she notice . 

 " I know what you want I to tell you , " say Colin , after she have star a few minute . " I always know when you want I to tell you something . you be wonder why the curtain be draw back . I be go to keep it like that . " 

 " why ? " ask Mary . 

 " because it do not   make I angry any more to see her laughing . I waken when it be bright moonlight two night ago and feel as if the Magic be fill the room and make everything so splendid that I could not   lie still . I get up and look out of the window . the room be quite light and there be a patch of moonlight on the curtain and somehow that make I go and pull the cord . she look right down at I as if she be laugh because she be glad I be stand there . it make I like to look at she . I want to see she laugh like that all the time . I think she must have be a sort of magic person perhaps . " 

 " you be so like she now , " say Mary , " that sometimes I think perhaps you be her ghost make into a boy . " 

 that idea seem to impress Colin . he think it over and then answer she slowly . 

 " if I be her ghost my father would be fond of I . " 

 " do you want he to be fond of you ? " inquire Mary . 

 " I use to hate it because he be not fond of I . if he grow fond of I I think I should tell he about the Magic . it might make he more cheerful . " 




 CHAPTER XXVI 

 " IT be mother ! " 

 their belief in the Magic be an abide thing . after the morning 's incantation Colin sometimes give they Magic lecture . 

 " I like to do it , " he explain , " because when I grow up and make great scientific discovery I shall be oblige to lecture about they and so this be practise . I can only give short lecture now because I be very young , and besides Ben Weatherstaff would feel as if he be in church and he would go to sleep . " 

 " Th ' good thing about lecturin ' , " say Ben , " be that a chap can get up an ' say aught he please an ' no other chap can answer he back . I would not   be agen ' lecturin ' a bit mysel ' sometimes . " 

 but when Colin hold forth under his tree old Ben fix devour eye on he and keep they there . he look he over with critical affection . it be not so much the lecture which interest he as the leg which look straighter and strong each day , the boyish head which hold itself up so well , the once sharp chin and hollow cheek which have fill and round out and the eye which have begin to hold the light he remember in another pair . sometimes when Colin feel Ben 's earnest gaze mean that he be much impressed he wonder what he be reflect on and once when he have seem quite entrance he question he . 

 " what be you think about , Ben Weatherstaff ? " he ask . 

 " I be thinkin ' " answer Ben , " as I would warrant tha 's , go up three or four pound this week . I be lookin ' at tha ' calve an ' tha ' shoulder . I would like to get thee on a pair o ' scale . " 

 " it be the Magic and and Mrs. Sowerby 's bun and milk and thing , " say Colin . " you see the scientific experiment have succeed . " 

 that morning Dickon be too late to hear the lecture . when he come he be ruddy with run and his funny face look more twinkle than usual . as they have a good deal of weed to do after the rain they fall to work . they always have plenty to do after a warm deep sink rain . the moisture which be good for the flower be also good for the weed which thrust up tiny blade of grass and point of leaf which must be pull up before their root take too firm hold . Colin be as good at weed as any one in these day and he could lecture while he be do it . " the Magic work well when you work , yourself , " he say this morning . " you can feel it in your bone and muscle . I be go to read book about bone and muscle , but I be go to write a book about Magic . I be make it up now . I keep find out thing . " 

 it be not very long after he have say this that he lay down his trowel and stand up on his foot . he have be silent for several minute and they have see that he be think out lecture , as he often do . when he drop his trowel and stand upright it seem to Mary and Dickon as if a sudden strong thought have make he do it . he stretch himself out to his tall height and he throw out his arm exultantly . color glow in his face and his strange eye widen with joyfulness . all at once he have realize something to the full . 

 " Mary ! Dickon ! " he cry . " just look at I ! " 

 they stop their weed and look at he . 

 " do you remember that first morning you bring I in here ? " he demand . 

 Dickon be look at he very hard . be an animal charmer he could see more thing than most people could and many of they be thing he never talk about . he see some of they now in this boy . " Aye , that we do , " he answer . 

 Mary look hard too , but she say nothing . 

 " just this minute , " say Colin , " all at once I remember it myself when I look at my hand dig with the trowel and I have to stand up on my foot to see if it be real . and it be real ! I be well I be well ! " 

 " Aye , that th ' art ! " say Dickon . 

 " I be well ! I be well ! " say Colin again , and his face go quite red all over . 

 he have know it before in a way , he have hop it and feel it and think about it , but just at that minute something have rush all through he a sort of rapturous belief and realization and it have be so strong that he could not help call out . 

 " I shall live forever and ever and ever ! " he cry grandly . " I shall find out thousand and thousand of thing . I shall find out about people and creature and everything that grow like Dickon and I shall never stop make Magic . I be well ! I be well ! I feel I feel as if I want to shout out something something thankful , joyful ! " 

 Ben Weatherstaff , who have be work near a rose - bush , glance round at he . 

 " Tha ' might sing th ' doxology , " he suggest in his dry grunt . he have no opinion of the Doxology and he do not make the suggestion with any particular reverence . 

 but Colin be of an explore mind and he know nothing about the Doxology . 

 " what be that ? " he inquire . 

 " Dickon can sing it for thee , I will warrant , " reply Ben Weatherstaff . 

 Dickon answer with his all - perceive animal charmer 's smile . 

 " they sing it I ' church , " he say . " mother say she believe th ' skylark sing it when they get up I ' th ' mornin ' . " 

 " if she say that , it must be a nice song , " Colin answer . " I have   never be in a church myself . I be always too ill . sing it , Dickon . I want to hear it . " 

 Dickon be quite simple and unaffected about it . he understand what Colin feel well than Colin do himself . he understand by a sort of instinct so natural that he do not know it be understand . he pull off his cap and look round still smile . 

 " Tha ' must take off tha ' cap , " he say to Colin , " an ' so mun tha ' , Ben an ' tha ' mun stand up , tha ' know . " 

 Colin take off his cap and the sun shine on and warm his thick hair as he watch Dickon intently . Ben Weatherstaff scramble up from his knee and bar his head too with a sort of puzzled half - resentful look on his old face as if he do not   know exactly why he be do this remarkable thing . 

 Dickon stand out among the tree and rose - bush and begin to sing in quite a simple matter - of - fact way and in a nice strong boy voice : 

 " praise God from whom all blessing flow , 
 praise he all creature here below , 
 praise he above ye Heavenly Host , 
 Praise Father , Son , and Holy Ghost . 
  amen . " 
 when he have finish , Ben Weatherstaff be stand quite still with his jaw set obstinately but with a disturbed look in his eye fix on Colin . Colin 's face be thoughtful and appreciative . 

 " it be a very nice song , " he say . " I like it . perhaps it mean just what I mean when I want to shout out that I be thankful to the Magic . " he stop and think in a puzzled way . " perhaps they be both the same thing . how can we know the exact name of everything ? sing it again , Dickon . let we try , Mary . I want to sing it , too . it be my song . how do it begin ? ' praise God from whom all blessing flow ' ? " 

 and they sing it again , and Mary and Colin lift their voice as musically as they could and Dickon 's swell quite loud and beautiful and at the second line Ben Weatherstaff raspingly clear his throat and at the third line he join in with such vigor that it seem almost savage and when the " amen " come to an end Mary observe that the very same thing have happen to he which have happen when he find out that Colin be not a cripple his chin be twitch and he be star and wink and his leathery old cheek be wet . 

 " I never seed no sense in th ' doxology afore , " he say hoarsely , " but I may change my mind I ' time . I should say tha'd go up five pound this week Mester Colin five on them ! " 

 Colin be look across the garden at something attract his attention and his expression have become a startled one . 

 " who be come in here ? " he say quickly . " who be it ? " 

 the door in the ivied wall have be push gently open and a woman have enter . she have come in with the last line of their song and she have stand still listen and look at they . with the ivy behind she , the sunlight drift through the tree and dapple her long blue cloak , and her nice fresh face smile across the greenery she be rather like a softly color illustration in one of Colin 's book . she have wonderful affectionate eye which seem to take everything in all of they , even Ben Weatherstaff and the " creature " and every flower that be in bloom . unexpectedly as she have appear , not one of they feel that she be an intruder at all . Dickon 's eye light like lamp . 

 " it be mother that be who it be ! " he cry and go across the grass at a run . 

 Colin begin to move toward she , too , and Mary go with he . they both feel their pulse beat fast . 

 " it be mother ! " Dickon say again when they meet halfway . " I know tha ' want to see she an ' I tell she where th ' door be hide . " 

 Colin hold out his hand with a sort of flushed royal shyness but his eye quite devour her face . 

 " even when I be ill I want to see you , " he say , " you and Dickon and the secret garden . I would never want to see any one or anything before . " 

 the sight of his uplifted face bring about a sudden change in her own . she flush and the corner of her mouth shake and a mist seem to sweep over her eye . 

 " eh ! dear lad ! " she break out tremulously . " eh ! dear lad ! " as if she have not know she be go to say it . she do not say , " Mester Colin , " but just " dear lad " quite suddenly . she might have say it to Dickon in the same way if she have see something in his face which touch she . Colin like it . 

 " be you surprised because I be so well ? " he ask . she put her hand on his shoulder and smile the mist out of her eye . " Aye , that I be ! " she say ; " but tha'rt so like thy mother tha ' make my heart jump . " 

 " do you think , " say Colin a little awkwardly , " that will make my father like I ? " 

 " Aye , for sure , dear lad , " she answer and she give his shoulder a soft quick pat . " he mun come home he mun come home . " 

 " Susan Sowerby , " say Ben Weatherstaff , get close to she . " look at th ' lad 's leg , wilt tha ' ? they be like drumstick I ' stockin ' two month ' ago an ' I hear folk tell as they be bandy an ' knock - kneed both at th ' same time . look at them now ! " 

 Susan Sowerby laugh a comfortable laugh . 

 " they be go to be fine strong lad 's leg in a bit , " she say . " let he go on playin ' an ' workin ' in the garden an ' eatin ' hearty an ' drinkin ' plenty o ' good sweet milk an ' there will not be a fine pair I ' yorkshire , thank God for it . " 

 she put both hand on Mistress Mary 's shoulder and look her little face over in a motherly fashion . 

 " an ' thee , too ! " she say . " Tha'rt grow near as hearty as our ' Lisabeth Ellen . I will warrant tha'rt like thy mother too . our Martha tell I as Mrs. Medlock hear she be a pretty woman . Tha'lt be like a blush rise when tha ' grow up , my little lass , bless thee . " 

 she do not mention that when Martha come home on her " day out " and describe the plain sallow child she have say that she have no confidence whatever in what Mrs. Medlock have hear . " it do not   stand to reason that a pretty woman could be th ' mother o ' such a fou ' little lass , " she have add obstinately . 

 Mary have not have time to pay much attention to her change face . she have only know that she look " different " and seem to have a great deal more hair and that it be grow very fast . but remember her pleasure in look at the Mem Sahib in the past she be glad to hear that she might some day look like she . 

 Susan Sowerby go round their garden with they and be tell the whole story of it and show every bush and tree which have come alive . Colin walk on one side of she and Mary on the other . each of they keep look up at her comfortable rosy face , secretly curious about the delightful feeling she give they a sort of warm , support feeling . it seem as if she understand they as Dickon understand his " creature . " she stoop over the flower and talk about they as if they be child . Soot follow she and once or twice caw at she and fly upon her shoulder as if it be Dickon 's . when they tell she about the robin and the first flight of the young one she laugh a motherly little mellow laugh in her throat . 

 " I suppose learnin ' them to fly be like learnin ' child to walk , but I be fear I should be all in a worrit if mine have wing instead o ' leg , " she say . 

 it be because she seem such a wonderful woman in her nice moorland cottage way that at last she be tell about the Magic . 

 " do you believe in Magic ? " ask Colin after he have explain about indian fakir . " I do hope you do . " 

 " that I do , lad , " she answer . " I never know it by that name but what do th ' name matter ? I warrant they call it a different name I ' France an ' a different one I ' Germany . th ' same thing as set th ' seed swellin ' an ' th ' sun shinin ' make thee a well lad an ' it be th ' Good Thing . it be not   like we poor fool as think it matter if we be call out of our name . Th ' Big Good Thing do not   stop to worrit , bless thee . it go on makin ' world by th ' million world like we . never thee stop believin ' in th ' Big Good Thing an ' knowin ' th ' world 's full of it an ' call it what tha ' like . tha ' wert singin ' to it when I come into th ' garden . " 

 " I feel so joyful , " say Colin , open his beautiful strange eye at she . " suddenly I feel how different I be how strong my arm and leg be , you know and how I could dig and stand and I jump up and want to shout out something to anything that would listen . " 

 " Th ' Magic listen when tha ' sing th ' Doxology . it would ha ' listen to anything tha'd sing . it be th ' joy that matter . eh ! lad , lad what be name to th ' Joy Maker , " and she give his shoulder a quick soft pat again . 

 she have pack a basket which hold a regular feast this morning , and when the hungry hour come and Dickon bring it out from its hiding place , she sit down with they under their tree and watch they devour their food , laugh and quite gloating over their appetite . she be full of fun and make they laugh at all sort of odd thing . she tell they story in broad Yorkshire and teach they new word . she laugh as if she could not help it when they tell she of the increase difficulty there be in pretend that Colin be still a fretful invalid . 

 " you see we can not   help laugh nearly all the time when we be together , " explain Colin . " and it do not   sound ill at all . we try to choke it back but it will burst out and that sound bad than ever . " 

 " there be one thing that come into my mind so often , " say Mary , " and I can scarcely ever hold in when I think of it suddenly . I keep think suppose Colin 's face should get to look like a full moon . it be not   like one yet but he get a tiny bit fatter every day and suppose some morning it should look like one what should we do ! " 

 " bless we all , I can see tha ' have a good bit o ' play actin ' to do , " say Susan Sowerby . " but tha ' will not   have to keep it up much long . Mester Craven'll come home . " 

 " do you think he will ? " ask Colin . " why ? " 

 Susan Sowerby chuckle softly . 

 " I suppose it ' ud nigh break thy heart if he find out before tha ' tell he in tha ' own way , " she say . " Tha 's lay awake night plannin ' it . "

" " that would be a fine start for he , " say Susan Sowerby . " I would like to see his face , lad . I would that ! he mun come back that he mun . " 

 one of the thing they talk of be the visit they be to make to her cottage . they plan it all . they be to drive over the moor and lunch out of door among the heather . they would see all the twelve child and Dickon 's garden and would not come back until they be tired . 

 Susan Sowerby get up at last to return to the house and Mrs. Medlock . it be time for Colin to be wheel back also . but before he get into his chair he stand quite close to Susan and fix his eye on she with a kind of bewildered adoration and he suddenly catch hold of the fold of her blue cloak and hold it fast .

 " eh ! dear lad ! " she say . " thy own mother 's in this ' ere very garden , I do believe . she couldna ' keep out of it . Thy father mun come back to thee he mun ! " 




 CHAPTER XXVII 

 in the GARDEN 

 in each century since the beginning of the world wonderful thing have be discover . in the last century more amazing thing be find out than in any century before . in this new century hundred of thing still more astounding will be bring to light . at first people refuse to believe that a strange new thing can be do , then they begin to hope it can be do , then they see it can be do then it be do and all the world wonder why it be not do century ago . one of the new thing people begin to find out in the last century be that thought just mere thought be as powerful as electric battery as good for one as sunlight be , or as bad for one as poison . to let a sad thought or a bad one get into your mind be as dangerous as let a scarlet fever germ get into your body . if you let it stay there after it have get in you may never get over it as long as you live . 

 so long as Mistress Mary 's mind be full of disagreeable thought about her dislike and sour opinion of people and her determination not to be please by or interested in anything , she be a yellow - faced , sickly , bored and wretched child . circumstance , however , be very kind to she , though she be not at all aware of it . they begin to push she about for her own good . when her mind gradually fill itself with robin , and moorland cottage crowd with child , with queer crab old gardener and common little Yorkshire housemaid , with springtime and with secret garden come alive day by day , and also with a moor boy and his " creature , " there be no room leave for the disagreeable thought which affect her liver and her digestion and make she yellow and tired . 

 so long as Colin shut himself up in his room and think only of his fear and weakness and his detestation of people who look at he and reflect hourly on hump and early death , he be a hysterical half - crazy little hypochondriac who know nothing of the sunshine and the spring and also do not know that he could get well and could stand upon his foot if he try to do it . when new beautiful thought begin to push out the old hideous one , life begin to come back to he , his blood run healthily through his vein and strength pour into he like a flood . his scientific experiment be quite practical and simple and there be nothing weird about it at all . much more surprising thing can happen to any one who , when a disagreeable or discouraged thought come into his mind , just have the sense to remember in time and push it out by put in an agreeable determinedly courageous one . two thing can not be in one place . 

 " where , you tend a rose , my lad , 
 a thistle can not grow . " 
 while the secret garden be come alive and two child be come alive with it , there be a man wander about certain far - away beautiful place in the norwegian fiord and the valley and mountain of Switzerland and he be a man who for ten year have keep his mind fill with dark and heart - break thinking . he have not be courageous ; he have never try to put any other thought in the place of the dark one . he have wander by blue lake and think they ; he have lain on mountain - side with sheet of deep blue gentian bloom all about he and flower breath fill all the air and he have think they . a terrible sorrow have fall upon he when he have be happy and he have let his soul fill itself with blackness and have refuse obstinately to allow any rift of light to pierce through . he have forget and desert his home and his duty . when he travel about , darkness so brood over he that the sight of he be a wrong do to other people because it be as if he poison the air about he with gloom . Most stranger think he must be either half mad or a man with some hide crime on his soul . he , be a tall man with a draw face and crooked shoulder and the name he always enter on hotel register be , " Archibald Craven , Misselthwaite Manor , Yorkshire , England . " 

 he have travel far and wide since the day he see Mistress Mary in his study and tell she she might have she " bit of earth . " he have be in the most beautiful place in Europe , though he have remain nowhere more than a few day . he have choose the quiet and remotest spot . he have be on the top of mountain whose head be in the cloud and have look down on other mountain when the sun rise and touch they with such light as make it seem as if the world be just be bear . 

 but the light have never seem to touch himself until one day when he realize that for the first time in ten year a strange thing have happen . he be in a wonderful valley in the Austrian Tyrol and he have be walk alone through such beauty as might have lift , any man 's soul out of shadow . he have walk a long way and it have not lift his . but at last he have feel tired and have throw himself down to rest on a carpet of moss by a stream . it be a clear little stream which run quite merrily along on its narrow way through the luscious damp greenness . sometimes it make a sound rather like very low laughter as it bubble over and round stone . he see bird come and dip their head to drink in it and then flick their wing and fly away . it seem like a thing alive and yet its tiny voice make the stillness seem deeply . the valley be very , very still . 

 as he sit gaze into the clear running of the water , Archibald Craven gradually feel his mind and body both grow quiet , as quiet as the valley itself . he wonder if he be go to sleep , but he be not . he sit and gaze at the sunlit water and his eye begin to see thing grow at its edge . there be one lovely mass of blue forget - I - not grow so close to the stream that its leaf be wet and at these he find himself look as he remember he have look at such thing year ago . he be actually think tenderly how lovely it be and what wonder of blue its hundred of little blossom be . he do not know that just that simple thought be slowly fill his mind fill and fill it until other thing be softly push aside . it be as if a sweet clear spring have begin to rise in a stagnant pool and have rise and rise until at last it sweep the dark water away . but of course he do not think of this himself . he only know that the valley seem to grow quieter and quieter as he sit and star at the bright delicate blueness . he do not know how long he sit there or what be happen to he , but at last he move as if he be awakening and he get up slowly and stand on the moss carpet , draw a long , deep , soft breath and wonder at himself . something seem to have be unbind and release in he , very quietly . 

 " what be it ? " he say , almost in a whisper , and he pass his hand over his forehead . " I almost feel as if I be alive ! " 

 I do not know enough about the wonderfulness of undiscovered thing to be able to explain how this have happen to he . neither do any one else yet . he do not understand at all himself but he remember this strange hour month afterward when he be at Misselthwaite again and he find out quite by accident that on this very day Colin have cry out as he go into the secret garden : 

 " I be go to live forever and ever and ever ! " 

 the singular calmness remain with he the rest of the evening and he sleep a new reposeful sleep ; but it be not with he very long . he do not know that it could be keep . by the next night he have open the door wide to his dark thought and they have come troop and rush back . he leave the valley and go on his wandering way again . but , strange as it seem to he , there be minute sometimes half - hour when , without his knowing why , the black burden seem to lift itself again and he know he be a live man and not a dead one . slowly slowly for no reason that he know of he be " come alive " with the garden . 

 as the golden summer change into the deep golden autumn he go to the Lake of Como . there he find the loveliness of a dream . he spend his day upon the crystal blueness of the lake or he walk back into the soft thick verdure of the hill and tramp until he be tired so that he might sleep . but by this time he have begin to sleep well , he know , and his dream have cease to be a terror to he . 

 " perhaps , " he think , " my body be grow strong . " 

 it be grow strong but because of the rare peaceful hour when his thought be change his soul be slowly grow strong , too . he begin to think of Misselthwaite and wonder if he should not go home . now and then he wonder vaguely about his boy and ask himself what he should feel when he go and stand by the carved four - post bed again and look down at the sharply chisel ivory - white face while it sleep and , the black lash rim so startlingly the close - shut eye . he shrink from it . 

 one marvel of a day he have walk so far that when he return the moon be high and full and all the world be purple shadow and silver . the stillness of lake and shore and wood be so wonderful that he do not go into the villa he live in . he walk down to a little bowered terrace at the water 's edge and sit upon a seat and breathe in all the heavenly scent of the night . he feel the strange calmness steal over he and it grow deep and deep until he fall asleep . 

 he do not know when he fall asleep and when he begin to dream ; his dream be so real that he do not feel as if he be dream . he remember afterward how intensely wide awake and alert he have think he be . he think that as he sit and breathe in the scent of the late rose and listen to the lapping of the water at his foot he hear a voice call . it be sweet and clear and happy and far away . it seem very far , but he hear it as distinctly as if it have be at his very side . 

 " Archie ! Archie ! Archie ! " it say , and then again , sweet and clear than before , " Archie ! Archie ! " 

 he think he spring to his foot not even startle . it be such a real voice and it seem so natural that he should hear it . 

 " Lilias ! Lilias ! " he answer . " Lilias ! where be you ? " 

 " in the garden , " it come back like a sound from a golden flute . " in the garden ! " 

 and then the dream end . but he do not awaken . he sleep soundly and sweetly all through the lovely night . when he do awake at last it be brilliant morning and a servant be stand star at he . he be an italian servant and be accustom , as all the servant of the villa be , to accept without question any strange thing his foreign master might do . no one ever know when he would go out or come in or where he would choose to sleep or if he would roam about the garden or lie in the boat on the lake all night . the man hold a salver with some letter on it and he wait quietly until Mr. Craven take they . when he have go away Mr. Craven sit a few moment hold they in his hand and look at the lake . his strange calm be still upon he and something more a lightness as if the cruel thing which have be do have not happen as he think as if something have change . he be remember the dream the real real dream . 

 " in the garden ! " he say , wonder at himself . " in the garden ! but the door be lock and the key be bury deep . " 

 when he glance at the letter a few minute later he see that the one lie at the top of the rest be an english letter and come from Yorkshire . it be direct in a plain woman 's hand but it be not a hand he know . he open it , scarcely think of the writer , but the first word attract his attention at once . 


 " Dear Sir : 

 I be Susan Sowerby that make bold to speak to you once on the moor . it be about Miss Mary I speak . I will make bold to speak again . please , sir , I would come home if I be you . I think you would be glad to come and if you will excuse I , sir I think your lady would ask you to come if she be here . 

 your obedient servant , 
  Susan Sowerby . " 

 Mr. Craven read the letter twice before he put it back in its envelope . he keep think about the dream . 

 " I will go back to Misselthwaite , " he say . " yes , I will go at once . " 

 and he go through the garden to the villa and order Pitcher to prepare for his return to England . 


 in a few day he be in Yorkshire again , and on his long railroad journey he find himself think of his boy as he have never think in all the ten year past . during those year he have only wish to forget he . now , though he do not intend to think about he , memory of he constantly drift into his mind . he remember the black day when he have rave like a madman because the child be alive and the mother be dead . he have refuse to see it , and when he have go to look at it at last it have be , such a weak wretched thing that everyone have be sure it would die in a few day . but to the surprise of those who take care of it the day pass and it live and then everyone believe it would be a deformed and crippled creature . 

 he have not mean to be a bad father , but he have not feel like a father at all . he have supply doctor and nurse and luxury , but he have shrink from the mere thought of the boy and have bury himself in his own misery . the first time after a year 's absence he return to Misselthwaite and the small miserable look thing languidly and indifferently lift to his face the great gray eye with black lash round they , so like and yet so horribly unlike the happy eye he have adore , he could not bear the sight of they and turn away pale as death . after that he scarcely ever see he except when he be asleep , and all he know of he be that he be a confirmed invalid , with a vicious , hysterical , half - insane temper . he could only be keep from fury dangerous to himself by be give his own way in every detail . 

 all this be not an uplifting thing to recall , but as the train whirl he through mountain pass and golden plain the man who be " come alive " begin to think in a new way and he think long and steadily and deeply . 

 " perhaps I have be all wrong for ten year , " he say to himself . " ten year be a long time . it may be too late to do anything quite too late . what have I be think of ! " 

 of course this be the wrong magic to begin by say " too late . " even Colin could have tell he that . but he know nothing of Magic either black or white . this he have yet to learn . he wonder if Susan Sowerby have take courage and write to he only because the motherly creature have realize that the boy be much bad be fatally ill . if he have not be under the spell of the curious calmness which have take possession of he he would have be more wretched than ever . but the calm have bring a sort of courage and hope with it . instead of give way to thought of the bad he actually find he be try to believe in well thing . 

 " could it be possible that she see that I may be able to do he good and control he ? " he think . " I will go and see she on my way to Misselthwaite . " 

 but when on his way across the moor he stop the carriage at the cottage , seven or eight child who be play about gather in a group and bob seven or eight friendly and polite curtsy tell he that their mother have go to the other side of the moor early in the morning to help a woman who have a new baby . " our Dickon , " they volunteer , be over at the Manor work in one of the garden where he go several day each week . 

 Mr. Craven look over the collection of sturdy little body and round red - cheeked face , each one grin in its own particular way , and he awake to the fact that they be a healthy likable lot . he smile at their friendly grin and take a golden sovereign from his pocket and give it to " our ' Lizabeth Ellen " who be the old . 

 " if you divide that into eight part there will be half a crown for each of , you , " he say . 

 then amid grin and chuckle and bob of curtsy he drive away , leave ecstasy and nudging elbow and little jump of joy behind . 

 the drive across the wonderfulness of the moor be a soothe thing . why do it seem to give he a sense of homecoming which he have be sure he could never feel again that sense of the beauty of land and sky and purple bloom of distance and a warming of the heart at drawing , near to the great old house which have hold those of his blood for six hundred year ? how he have drive away from it the last time , shudder to think of its close room and the boy lie in the four - post bed with the brocade hanging . be it possible that perhaps he might find he change a little for the well and that he might overcome his shrinking from he ? how real that dream have be how wonderful and clear the voice which call back to he , " in the garden in the garden ! " 

 " I will try to find the key , " he say . " I will try to open the door . I must though I do not   know why . " 

 when he arrive at the Manor the servant who receive he with the usual ceremony notice that he look well and that he do not go to the remote room where he usually live attend by Pitcher . he go into the library and send for Mrs. Medlock . she come to he somewhat excited and curious and fluster . 

 " how be Master Colin , Medlock ? " he inquire . " well , sir , " Mrs. Medlock answer , " he be he be different , in a manner of speak . " 

 " bad ? " he suggest . 

 Mrs. Medlock really be flushed . 

 " well , you see , sir , " she try to explain , " neither Dr. Craven , nor the nurse , nor I can exactly make he out . " 

 " why be that ? " 

 " to tell the truth , sir , Master Colin might be well and he might be change for the bad . his appetite , sir , be past understanding and his way " 

 " have he become more more peculiar ? " her master , ask , knit his brow anxiously . 

 " that be it , sir . he be grow very peculiar when you compare he with what he use to be . he use to eat nothing and then suddenly he begin to eat something enormous and then he stop again all at once and the meal be send back just as they use to be . you never know , sir , perhaps , that out of door he never would let himself be take . the thing we have   go through to get he to go out in his chair would leave a body tremble like a leaf . he would throw himself into such a state that Dr. Craven say he could not   be responsible for force he . well , sir , just without warn not long after one of his bad tantrum he suddenly insist on be take out every day by Miss Mary and Susan Sowerby 's boy Dickon that could push his chair . he take a fancy to both Miss Mary and Dickon , and Dickon bring his tame animal , and , if you will credit it , sir , out of door he will stay from morning until night . " 

 " how do he look ? " be the next question . 

 " if he take his food natural , sir , you would think he be put on flesh but we be afraid it may be a sort of bloat . he laugh sometimes in a queer way when he be alone with Miss Mary . he never use to laugh at all . Dr. Craven be come to see you at once , if you will allow he . he never be as puzzle in his life . " 

 " where be Master Colin now ? " Mr. Craven ask . 

 " in the garden , sir . he be always in the garden though not a human creature be allow to go near for fear they will look at he . " 

 Mr. Craven scarcely hear her last word . 

 " in the garden , " he say , and after he have send Mrs. Medlock away he stand and repeat it again and again . " in the garden ! " 

 he have to make an effort to bring himself back to the place he be stand in and when he feel he be on earth again he turn and go out of the room . he take his way , as Mary have do , through the door in the shrubbery and among the laurel and the fountain bed . the fountain be play now and be encircle by bed of brilliant autumn flower . he cross the lawn and turn into the Long Walk by the ivied wall . he do not walk quickly , but slowly , and his eye be on the path . he feel as if he be be draw back to the place he have so long forsaken , and he do not know why . as he draw near to it his step become still more slow . he know where the door be even though the ivy hang thick over it but he do not know exactly where it lie that bury key .

" who what ? who ! " he stammer .

Mary , who have be run with he and have dash through the door too , believe that he manage to make himself look tall than he have ever look before inch tall . 

 " Father , " he say , " I be Colin . you can not   believe it . I scarcely can myself . I be Colin . "

 " in the garden ! in the garden ! "

 he say it all so like a healthy boy his face flush , his word tumble over each other in his eagerness that Mr. Craven 's soul shake with unbelieving joy .

 and so they lead he in . 

 the place be a wilderness of autumn gold and purple and violet blue and flame scarlet and on every side be sheaf of late lily stand together lily which be white or white and ruby . he remember well when the first of they have be plant that just at this season of the year their late glory should reveal themselves . late rose climb and hang and cluster and the sunshine deepen the hue of the yellowing tree make one feel that one , stand in an embowered temple of gold . the newcomer stand silent just as the child have do when they come into its grayness . he look round and round . 

 " I think it would be dead , " he say . 

 " Mary think so at first , " say Colin . " but it come alive . " 

 then they sit down under their tree all but Colin , who want to stand while he tell the story . 

 it be the strange thing he have ever hear , Archibald Craven think , as it be pour forth in headlong boy fashion . mystery and Magic and wild creature , the weird midnight meet the coming of the spring the passion of insult pride which have drag the young Rajah to his foot to defy old Ben Weatherstaff to his face . the odd companionship , the play acting , the great secret so carefully keep . the listener laugh until tear come into his eye and sometimes tear come into his eye when he be not laugh . the Athlete , the Lecturer , the scientific Discoverer be a laughable , lovable , healthy young human thing . 

 " now , " he say at the end of the story , " it need not be a secret any more . I dare say it will frighten they nearly into fit when they see I but I be never go to get into the chair again . I shall walk back with you , Father to the house . " 


 Ben Weatherstaff 's duty rarely take he away from the garden , but on this occasion he make an excuse to carry some vegetable to the kitchen and be invite into the servant ' hall by Mrs. Medlock to drink a glass of beer he be on the spot as he have hop to be when the most dramatic event Misselthwaite Manor have see during the present generation actually take place . one of the window look upon the courtyard give also a glimpse of the lawn . Mrs. Medlock , know Ben have come from the garden , hop that he might have catch sight of his master and even by chance of his meeting with Master Colin . 

 " do you see either of they , Weatherstaff ? " she ask . 

 Ben take his beer - mug from his mouth and wipe his lip with the back of his hand . 

 " Aye , that I do , " he answer with a shrewdly significant air . 

 " both of they ? " suggest Mrs. Medlock . 

 " both of them , " return Ben Weatherstaff . " thank ye kindly , ma'am , I could sup up another mug of it . " 

 " together ? " say Mrs. Medlock , hastily overfill his beer - mug in her excitement . 

 " together , ma'am , " and Ben gulp down half of his new mug at one gulp . 

 " where be Master Colin ? how do he look ? what do they say to each other ? " 

 " I didna ' hear that , " say Ben , " along o ' only bein ' on th ' stepladder lookin , over th ' wall . but I will tell thee this . there be be thing go on outside as you house people know nowt about . an ' what tha'll find out tha'll find out soon . " 

 and it be not two minute before he swallow the last of his beer and wave his mug solemnly toward the window which take in through the shrubbery a piece of the lawn . 

 " look there , " he say , " if tha 's curious . look what be comin ' across th ' grass . " 

 when Mrs. Medlock look she throw up her hand and give a little shriek and every man and woman servant within hearing bolt across the servant ' hall and stand look through the window with their eye almost start out of their head . 

 across the lawn come the Master of Misselthwaite and he look as many of they have never see he . and by his , side with his head up in the air and his eye full of laughter walk as strongly and steadily as any boy in Yorkshire Master Colin .
